 Let us know what things should be kept in mind while worshiping in Hinduism
 1
 What should be the right place of worship in the house - There should always be a temple in the east or north
 - ghar kaa mandir hameshaa lakdi kaa ho
 - There should be no dirt around the temple of the house
 2
 What is the main color of the temple of the house - the correct color of the temple is light yellow or orange
 - ghar ke mandir main hameshaa halki pili lite kaa prayog karnaa chahie
 - Do not use dark blue color in the temple
 3
 What should be kept in the house temple - Put a light colored yellow or red cloth in the house temple
 - bhagwaan ganpati or mahalakshmi kaa swaroop rakhen
 - Keep a picture of your favorite and your total guru
 - ek tambe ke lote mengangajalbharkar rakhen
 4
 ghar kaa mandir banaate samay kya-kya saavdhaanee baraten-- ghar kaa mandir dakshin pashchim disha main nahin hona chahie
 - There should be no dirt around the temple
 - mandir shauchalay ke paas bilkul naa banaaen
 - Do not keep shoes around the temple 5
 koun si disha main baithkar bhajan kirthan jaap kiya jaae-- hameshaa bhajan kirthan purv yaa uttar disha main munh karke kiya jaae to sarvottam rahata he
 a hymn performed in any other direction does not bring enthusiasm in the mind
 - bhajan kirthan karne se pehle bhagwaan mangalamurtike chitra ko hameshaa sthapit karen or uske baad hi bhajan kirthan shuru karen
 - In front of the picture of the deity that is being worshiped, light a lamp and incense of cow ghee and keep a vessel of water
 6
 What are the precautions to be taken in Bhajan Kirtan - While chanting Bhajan, do not pay attention to things around here
 - hameshaa shuddh or saaf vastra pahanakar hi bhajan kirthan karen
 - Use pure sweets and clean fruits in Bhajan Kirtan
 - hameshaa bhajan kirthan main gaay ke ghi kaa deepak or kalave kii baaten kaa prayog karen
 7
 ghar main puja paath or jaap kaa puraa fal paane ke liye karen upaay-- ghar main puja paath karte samay shwet gulabi yaa halke pile vastra pahanakar hi puja karen
 - Always chant the mantra sitting on the red Yapilasan
 - jaap hameshaa laal chandan kii maala yaa rudraksh kii maala se karen
 - Before starting the chant, Lord Ganpati and Guru and your favorite should be meditated
 uske baad hi jaap shuru karen
 8
 har pareshaaniyon ko dur karne ke upaay-- ghar main akaaran kalah rahata ho to pratidin subah gayatrimantraka 108 baar jaap karen

 In 1962, this seat came under the control of Congress
 1967 main swatantra party ne seat par khaataa kholaa

 1977 main jab desh main congress ke khilaaf lahar bani to devendra satpathi bhartiya lok dal main aa gaye or is seat par chunaav jite
